Session Number: 74

Chapter: Chapter 5 : The Knight and the Dragon

Key Locations: Valherst

Glory Gains:

Players Attending:

# Synopsis

Casimer delves into discussions about power structures over a drink with Philippe Montague, the ex squire of Leon Blackwood. A revelation unfolds as Caden expresses his desire to kill Leon Blackwood during a conversation. Casimir engages in a philosophical discourse touching on breaking points, Louis Covingard, and the Ashen Knights. Philippe says that he is on his way to Pearstone.  
  
Peter is selected for a crucial mission, meeting Nykos, a spy embedded in Emmerich Bennet's retinue. Together, they concoct a plan to smuggle Nykos out among Shobhan's trunks. As they keep going to Valherst they see a hailstorm during their city exit unveils a deceptive display of wheat bundles concealing wood, possibly dating back to the Saffron War. Clearly showing that their entire experience has been curated.

Upon reaching the capital, the group discovers fruit baskets and suspicious holes in their rooms. Casimir encounters Robert Nyirborg, a respected figure among the the Montmer court, he is a Peacekeeper, in a training area. Attendees gather for the "Conversation of the Wise," with Siobhan, Caden, and Sovereign in attendance.

Siobhan engages in conversation with Charles and Lucy Montimier, while Tanya is expected to arrive with prisoners. Charles reflects on Lucy's state-mandated marriage but retains affection for his first wife. Sovereign speaks with Esmeralda Goyca, who lost an eye in the Makado Crusades.

Sarah is highlighted as a "shining star" in the Bellkind court. Conflicts arise between Pelist folks and locals, prompting military intervention. Zacariah attempts to halt a pogrom with limited success. Esmeralda Goyca reveals she lost her eye using a gun against the Mikado, causing it to melt.

Daphne leaves Leon for Sherman, with Endy being her first lover. Clarissa Upperton and Lyla explore wedding and suitor discussions, contemplating marriage prospects and considering Lyla's connection with House Rhelrya. Lyla contemplates a potential connection with House Rhelrya, specifically eyeing the son of Solara Rhelrya.
